/****** Object:  View [dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_VP_EXTRACT_FILTER_V]    Script Date: 11/24/2025 4:05:15 PM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE VIEW [dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_VP_EXTRACT_FILTER_V] 
AS 
SELECT * FROM [dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_VP_EXTRACT] VP
WHERE 
vp.RevEntity NOT IN ('HK89','VG18') AND
vp.MatterType NOT IN ('TN') AND
vp.New_S4_product IS NOT NULL AND
CAST(SUBSTRING(vp.ToDate,1,10) AS DATE) BETWEEN CAST('2023-01-01' AS DATE) AND CAST('2029-12-31' AS DATE) AND
CAST(SUBSTRING(vp.FromDate,1,10) AS DATE) BETWEEN CAST('2023-01-01' AS DATE) AND CAST('2029-12-31' AS DATE)
AND vp.Charge_Per NOT IN ('2 years')
GO
/****** Object:  View [dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_VP_DRE_DUMMY_V]    Script Date: 11/24/2025 4:05:15 PM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE VIEW [dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_VP_DRE_DUMMY_V]
AS 
SELECT [Master_File_Name]
      ,[Master_File_Code_ORIGINAL] AS [Master_File_Code]
      ,[File_status]
      ,[File_Type]
      ,[Block_Reason]
      ,[Client___Group_Code]
      ,[Client___Group_Name]
      ,[Send_Invoice_to]
      ,[Send_Invoice_Name]
      ,[File_Handler]
      ,[File_Handler_Name]
      ,[RelationShip_Manager]
      ,[RelationShip_Manager_Name]
      ,[Senior_Relationship_Manager]
      ,[Senior_Relationship_Manager_Name]
      ,[Standard_Payment_term]
      ,[Role_Indexation]
      ,[Administration_Mark_Up]
      ,[Billing_Filce_Notes]
      ,[Notes]
      ,[Note]
      ,[MatterCode]
      ,[Description]
      ,[MatterStatus]
      ,[Default]
      ,[Created]
      ,[DateClosed]
      ,[RateList]
      ,[Notes_1]
      ,[Invoice_through]
      ,[Invoice_Billing_File]
      ,[InvoiceMatter]
      ,MatterType
      ,RevEntity
      ,[RevEntity_Name]
      ,[Primary_Team]
      ,[invoice_Type]
      ,[Currency]
      ,[Bill_WIP_at_USD]
      ,[Fee_Number]
      ,[Matter]
      ,[Service_Code]
      ,[Legacy_Product]
      ,New_S4_product
      ,[Remarks]
      ,[Item_Category]
      ,[Rdescription]
      ,[Currency_1]
      ,[Charge_Per]
      ,[Numer_Of_Units]
      ,[UnitPrice]
      ,[DiscountPerc]
      ,[Discount_Amount]
      ,[Total_Fee]
      ,EffectDate
      ,NextDate
      ,[FromDate]
      ,[ToDate]
      ,[Last_Invoiced]
      ,[Date_Terminated]
      ,[Time_Charge_Amount_Eur]
      ,[Service_Country]
      ,[PROJECTS]
      ,[DUMMY]
  FROM [dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_VP_DRE_DUMMY] D
  CROSS JOIN
  (SELECT 
  DISTINCT [Master_File_Code] AS [Master_File_Code_original]
  FROM
  [dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_VP_EXTRACT_FILTER_V] vp
  ) E
GO
/****** Object:  Table [dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_BUDDY]    Script Date: 11/24/2025 4:05:15 PM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON

CREATE TABLE [dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_BUDDY](
	[JOIN_KEY] [nvarchar](1000) NULL,
	[SRC] [nvarchar](1000) NULL,
	[COMMENT] [nvarchar](1000) NULL,
	[Material_Number] [nvarchar](1000) NULL,
	[Work_Package_Name] [nvarchar](1000) NULL,
	[Profit_Center] [nvarchar](1000) NULL,
	[Sales_Document_Item_Category] [nvarchar](1000) NULL,
	[Start_Date_wp] [nvarchar](1000) NULL,
	[end_date_wp] [nvarchar](1000) NULL,
	[Calendar_Year] [nvarchar](1000) NULL,
	[Calendar_Month] [nvarchar](1000) NULL,
	[WP_Type] [nvarchar](1000) NULL,
	[Service_ID] [nvarchar](1000) NULL,
	[Service_Quantity] [nvarchar](1000) NULL
) ON [PRIMARY]
GO
/****** Object:  View [dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_VP_BUDDY_V]    Script Date: 11/24/2025 4:05:15 PM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE   VIEW [dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_VP_BUDDY_V] AS
SELECT 
       [Master_File_Name]
      ,[Master_File_Code]
      ,[File_status]
      ,[File_Type]
      ,[Block_Reason]
      ,[Client___Group_Code]
      ,[Client___Group_Name]
      ,[Send_Invoice_to]
      ,[Send_Invoice_Name]
      ,[File_Handler]
      ,[File_Handler_Name]
      ,[RelationShip_Manager]
      ,[RelationShip_Manager_Name]
      ,[Senior_Relationship_Manager]
      ,[Senior_Relationship_Manager_Name]
      ,[Standard_Payment_term]
      ,[Role_Indexation]
      ,[Administration_Mark_Up]
      ,[Billing_Filce_Notes]
      ,[Notes]
      ,[Note]
      ,[MatterCode]
      ,[Description]
      ,[MatterStatus]
      ,[Default]
      ,[Created]
      ,[DateClosed]
      ,[RateList]
      ,[Notes_1]
      ,[Invoice_through]
      ,[Invoice_Billing_File]
      ,[InvoiceMatter]
      ,MatterType
      ,RevEntity
      ,[RevEntity_Name]
      ,[Primary_Team]
      ,[invoice_Type]
      ,[Currency]
      ,[Bill_WIP_at_USD]
      ,[Fee_Number]
      ,[Matter]
      ,[Service_Code]
      ,[Legacy_Product]
      ,b.MATERIAL_NUMBER AS New_S4_product
      ,[Remarks]
      ,b.sales_document_item_category AS [Item_Category]
      ,b.work_package_name AS [Work_Package_Name]
      ,[Currency_1]
      ,[Charge_Per]
      ,[Numer_Of_Units]
      ,[UnitPrice]
      ,[DiscountPerc]
      ,[Discount_Amount]
      ,[Total_Fee]
      ,CONVERT(VARCHAR(10), cast(Start_Date_wp as date), 120) AS EffectDate
      ,NextDate
      ,[FromDate]
      ,[ToDate]
      ,[Last_Invoiced]
      ,[Date_Terminated]
      ,[Time_Charge_Amount_Eur]
      ,[Service_Country]
      ,[PROJECTS]
      ,[DUMMY]
FROM
DBO.[SAP_IN_PROJECT_VP_EXTRACT_FILTER_V] VP
INNER JOIN
(
SELECT * 
FROM [dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_BUDDY]
WHERE SRC LIKE 'CLONE_BUDDY%'
) B
ON VP.New_S4_product=B.JOIN_KEY
GO

/****** Object:  View [dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_SC_V2_FILTER_V]    Script Date: 11/24/2025 4:05:15 PM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE         VIEW [dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_SC_V2_FILTER_V] 
AS 
SELECT [Transaction_ID]
      ,[Item_Number_in_Doc_]
	  ,'PS06' item_category
      ,Product_item
	  ,P.NEW_PRODUCT
      ,[Product_Description_item]
      ,[Ship_To_Party_header]
      ,[Bill_To_Party_Header]
      ,[Payer_Header]
      ,[Sold_To_Party_Header]
      ,[Net_Value_item_1]
      ,[Ship_To_Party_item]
      ,[Bill_To_Party_item]
      ,[Sold_To_Party_item]
      ,[Payer_item]
      ,[Settlement_End]
      ,[Settlement_Start]
      ,Contract_Start_Date_item
      ,Item_Category_item
      ,Life_Cycle_Status_item_1
      ,[Currency_Header]
	  ,Execution_Country
FROM 
(
SELECT SC.* 
 FROM 
[dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_SC_V2] SC
WHERE Life_Cycle_Status_item_1 <> 'C' AND 
SUBSTRING(Contract_Start_Date_item,1,10) BETWEEN '20230101' AND '20291231' AND
--SUBSTRING(Contract_End_Date_item,1,10) > '20250931' AND
Item_Category_item IN ('SCN2','SCN1') AND 
[Transaction_ID] IN
(SELECT distinct H.Service_Contract
FROM 
[dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_SC_HEADER] h
WHERE H.life_cycle_status = 'Released'
) AND 
SC.[Transaction_ID]  IN (SELECT F.SERVICE_CONTRACT FROM [dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_SC_FILTER] F)
) SC
INNER JOIN [dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_SC_PRODUCT] P
ON P.LEGACY_PRODUCT = SC.Product_item AND
P.NEW_PRODUCT IS NOT NULL 
--AND SC.[Transaction_ID] = '7000016157'



GO
/****** Object:  View [dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_SC_DRE_V]    Script Date: 11/24/2025 4:05:15 PM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE VIEW [dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_SC_DRE_V] AS
SELECT sc.[Transaction_ID]
      ,sc.[Item_Number_in_Doc_]
      ,dre.Sales_Document_Item_Category AS [item_category]
      ,CAST(NULL AS VARCHAR) AS [Product_item]
      ,dre.Material_Number AS [NEW_PRODUCT]
      ,dre.Work_Package_Name AS [Product_Description_item]
      ,CAST(NULL AS VARCHAR) AS [Ship_To_Party_header]
      ,CAST(NULL AS VARCHAR) AS [Bill_To_Party_Header]
      ,CAST(NULL AS VARCHAR) AS [Payer_Header]
      ,CAST(NULL AS VARCHAR) AS [Sold_To_Party_Header]
      ,CAST(NULL AS VARCHAR) AS [Net_Value_item_1]
      ,CAST(NULL AS VARCHAR) AS [Ship_To_Party_item]
      ,CAST(NULL AS VARCHAR) AS [Bill_To_Party_item]
      ,CAST(NULL AS VARCHAR) AS [Sold_To_Party_item]
      ,CAST(NULL AS VARCHAR) AS [Payer_item]
      ,CAST(NULL AS VARCHAR) AS [Settlement_End]
      ,dre.Start_Date_wp AS [Settlement_Start]
      ,dre.Start_Date_wp AS [Contract_Start_Date_item]
      ,'SCN1' AS [Item_Category_item]
      ,'D' AS [Life_Cycle_Status_item_1]
      ,CAST(NULL AS VARCHAR) AS [Currency_Header]
      ,CAST(NULL AS VARCHAR) AS [Execution_Country]
FROM
(
SELECT Transaction_ID,MIN(ITEM_NUMBER_IN_DOC_) ITEM_NUMBER_IN_DOC_
FROM
[dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_SC_V2_FILTER_V]
GROUP BY Transaction_ID
) sc
CROSS JOIN
(
SELECT Material_Number,Work_Package_Name,Sales_Document_Item_Category,CONVERT(VARCHAR,CAST(Start_Date_wp AS DATE),112) Start_Date_wp
FROM [dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_BUDDY]
WHERE JOIN_KEY = 'CLONE_DRE'
) dre
GO
/****** Object:  View [dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_SC_BUDDY_V]    Script Date: 11/24/2025 4:05:15 PM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE VIEW [dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_SC_BUDDY_V] AS
SELECT sc.[Transaction_ID]
      ,sc.[Item_Number_in_Doc_]
      ,b.Sales_Document_Item_Category AS [item_category]
      ,sc.[Product_item]
      ,b.Material_Number AS [NEW_PRODUCT]
      ,b.Work_Package_Name AS [Product_Description_item]
      ,sc.[Ship_To_Party_header]
      ,sc.[Bill_To_Party_Header]
      ,sc.[Payer_Header]
      ,sc.[Sold_To_Party_Header]
      ,sc.[Net_Value_item_1]
      ,sc.[Ship_To_Party_item]
      ,sc.[Bill_To_Party_item]
      ,sc.[Sold_To_Party_item]
      ,sc.[Payer_item]
      ,sc.[Settlement_End]
      ,sc.[Settlement_Start]
      ,sc.[Contract_Start_Date_item]
      ,sc.[Item_Category_item]
      ,sc.[Life_Cycle_Status_item_1]
      ,sc.[Currency_Header]
      ,sc.[Execution_Country]
FROM
(
SELECT *
FROM
[dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_SC_V2_FILTER_V]
) sc
INNER JOIN
(
SELECT 
b.*
FROM [dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_BUDDY] b
WHERE src like '%BUDDY%'
) b
ON sc.new_product = b.JOIN_KEY
GO

	[Product] ASC

/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_SC_BILLING_PRC]    Script Date: 11/24/2025 4:05:16 PM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE   PROCEDURE [dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_SC_BILLING_PRC]
AS
BEGIN

SET NOCOUNT ON;

DECLARE
@p1 VARCHAR(100),@p2 VARCHAR(100),@p3 VARCHAR(100),@p4 VARCHAR(100),@p5 VARCHAR(100),@p6 VARCHAR(100),
@p7 VARCHAR(100),@p8 VARCHAR(100),@p9 VARCHAR(100),@p10 VARCHAR(100),@p11 VARCHAR(100),@p12 VARCHAR(100);

DECLARE VP_CURSOR CURSOR FOR 
SELECT 
commercial_project_id, --1,
item_number_of_the_SD_document,--2
'dummy_sequence' dummy_seq, --3,
'dummy_billing_date' dummy_billing_date, --4,
CASE WHEN item_category IN ('PS02','PS07') THEN 1
     WHEN item_category IN ('PS01','PS06') THEN
            CASE WHEN frequency IN ('Tri-Annually') THEN ROUND(CAST(Net_Value_item_1 AS FLOAT)/4,2)
	        WHEN frequency IN ('Half Yearly') THEN ROUND(CAST(Net_Value_item_1 AS FLOAT)/6,2)
	        ELSE CAST(Net_Value_item_1 AS FLOAT)
            END
END AS Net_Value_in_Document_Currency,--5
START_DATE_ETL Service_Start_Date_ETL,--6
--DATEADD(YEAR,1,CAST(SUBSTRING(CASE WHEN SRC = 'DRE' THEN start_date_wp_etl ELSE fromdate END,1,10) AS DATE)) Service_Start_Date_ETL,
END_DATE_WP_ETL Service_End_Date_ETL,--7
material_number,--8
wp_description,--9
item_category AS sales_document_item_category,--10
src,--11,
frequency --12
--start_date_wp_etl,fromdate,todate,charge_per,total_fee
FROM 
[dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_SC_STG] 
WHERE name_for_date_rule IS NOT NULL;


TRUNCATE TABLE [dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_SC_BILLING_STG];

OPEN VP_CURSOR;

FETCH NEXT FROM VP_CURSOR INTO @P1,@P2,@P3,@P4,@P5,@P6,@P7,@P8,@P9,@P10,@P11,@P12;

WHILE @@FETCH_STATUS = 0
BEGIN

	IF @P12 IN ('One Off')
	BEGIN
	      INSERT INTO [dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_SC_BILLING_STG]
		  SELECT @P1,@P2,'1',@P6,@P5,@P6,@P7,@P8,@P9,@P10,@P11,@P12;
	END

   ELSE IF @P12 IN ('Annually')
	BEGIN
     WITH DateList AS (
       SELECT CAST(@P6 AS DATE) AS START_DT
       UNION ALL
       SELECT DATEADD(YEAR, 1, START_DT)
       FROM DateList
       WHERE CAST(START_DT AS DATE) < CAST(@P7 AS DATE)
     )
     INSERT INTO [dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_SC_BILLING_STG]
	 SELECT @P1,@P2,'1',START_DT,@P5,START_DT,DATEADD(DAY,-1,DATEADD(YEAR, 1, START_DT)),@P8,@P9,@P10,@P11,@P12
     FROM DateList
	 WHERE DATEADD(DAY,-1,DATEADD(YEAR, 1, START_DT)) <= CAST(@P7 AS DATE)
    OPTION (MAXRECURSION 0);
	END 
	ELSE IF @P12 IN ('Quarterly')
	BEGIN
     WITH DateList AS (
       SELECT CAST(@P6 AS DATE) AS START_DT
       UNION ALL
       SELECT DATEADD(QUARTER, 1, START_DT)
       FROM DateList
       WHERE CAST(START_DT AS DATE) < CAST(@P7 AS DATE)
     )
     INSERT INTO [dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_SC_BILLING_STG]
	 SELECT @P1,@P2,'1',DATEADD(DAY,-1,DATEADD(QUARTER, 1, START_DT)),@P5,START_DT,DATEADD(DAY,-1,DATEADD(QUARTER, 1, START_DT)),@P8,@P9,@P10,@P11,@P12
     FROM DateList
	 WHERE DATEADD(DAY,-1,DATEADD(QUARTER, 1, START_DT)) <= CAST(@P7 AS DATE)
    OPTION (MAXRECURSION 0);
	END

   ELSE --Monthly and others
	BEGIN
     WITH DateList AS (
       SELECT CAST(@P6 AS DATE) AS START_DT
       UNION ALL
       SELECT DATEADD(MONTH, 1, START_DT)
       FROM DateList
       WHERE CAST(START_DT AS DATE) < CAST(@P7 AS DATE)
     )
     INSERT INTO [dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_SC_BILLING_STG]
	 SELECT @P1,@P2,'1',DATEADD(DAY,-1,DATEADD(MONTH, 1, START_DT)),@P5,START_DT,DATEADD(DAY,-1,DATEADD(MONTH, 1, START_DT)),@P8,@P9,@P10,@P11,@P12
     FROM DateList
	 WHERE DATEADD(DAY,-1,DATEADD(MONTH, 1, START_DT)) <= CAST(@P7 AS DATE)
    OPTION (MAXRECURSION 0);

	END

FETCH NEXT FROM VP_CURSOR INTO @P1,@P2,@P3,@P4,@P5,@P6,@P7,@P8,@P9,@P10,@P11,@P12;

END

CLOSE VP_CURSOR;
DEALLOCATE VP_CURSOR;

END



GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_SC_PRC]    Script Date: 11/24/2025 4:05:16 PM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE           PROCEDURE [dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_SC_PRC] 
AS

BEGIN

TRUNCATE TABLE dbo.SAP_IN_PROJECT_SC_STG;

--drop table dbo.SAP_IN_PROJECT_SC_STG;

INSERT INTO dbo.SAP_IN_PROJECT_SC_STG
SELECT DISTINCT 
COUNT(*) OVER (PARTITION BY Commercial_Project_ID,Work_Package_Name_ETL) work_package_dup,
CAST(DENSE_RANK() OVER (PARTITION BY Commercial_Project_ID ORDER BY Commercial_Project_ID,Item_Number_in_Doc_key,Work_Package_Name_ETL,material_number,contract_start_date_item)  AS VARCHAR(100))   AS Sequence_Number,
CAST(DENSE_RANK() OVER (PARTITION BY Commercial_Project_ID ORDER BY Commercial_Project_ID,Item_Number_in_Doc_key,Work_Package_Name_ETL,material_number,contract_start_date_item)  AS VARCHAR(100))   AS Item_Number_of_the_SD_Document,
CONVERT(VARCHAR,CAST(MIN(Start_Date_ETL) OVER (PARTITION BY Commercial_Project_ID)AS DATE),104) Start_Date,
billing.CRM__Order_Quantity,
billing.Name_for_Date_Rule,
billing.frequency,
B.*
--INTO dbo.SAP_IN_PROJECT_SC_STG
FROM
(
SELECT DISTINCT 'M1'+v2.Transaction_ID AS Commercial_Project_ID,
v2.Item_Number_in_Doc_ AS Item_Number_in_Doc_key,
xref.customer_new AS Customer_ID,
'M1'+CASE WHEN V2.NEW_PRODUCT='DISB0002PFP' THEN 'FAAMAT081PPS' ELSE V2.NEW_PRODUCT END AS Material_Number,
CASE WHEN v2.item_category IN ('PS07') THEN 'U' ELSE NULL END AS WP_Type,
CASE WHEN v2.item_category IN ('PS07') THEN 'U003' ELSE NULL END AS Service_ID,
CASE WHEN v2.item_category IN ('PS07') THEN '1' ELSE NULL END AS Service_Quantity,
LEFT(CASE WHEN v2.[Product_Description_item] IS NULL OR TRIM(v2.[Product_Description_item])='N/A' THEN h.Project_Name ELSE v2.[Product_Description_item] END,58) AS Work_Package_Name_ETL,
CASE WHEN v2.[Product_Description_item] IS NULL OR TRIM(v2.[Product_Description_item])='N/A' THEN h.Project_Name ELSE v2.[Product_Description_item] END AS WP_Description,
CASE WHEN v2.[Product_Description_item] IS NULL OR TRIM(v2.[Product_Description_item])='N/A' THEN h.Project_Name ELSE v2.[Product_Description_item] END AS Material_Description,
CASE WHEN V2.execution_country IS NULL THEN 'GB' ELSE V2.execution_country END AS Price_Refresh___Country,
CASE WHEN V2.execution_country IS NULL THEN 'GB' ELSE V2.execution_country END AS CDM,
v2.Currency_Header AS Currency,
NULL Project_Manager_ID_ETL,
H.*,
CONVERT(VARCHAR,CAST(LEFT(V2.contract_start_date_item,8) AS DATE),104) Start_Date_WP,
CONVERT(VARCHAR,CAST(LEFT(V2.contract_start_date_item,8) AS DATE),23) Start_Date_ETL, 
SUBSTRING(V2.contract_start_date_item,1,4) Calendar_Year,
SUBSTRING(V2.contract_start_date_item,5,2) Calendar_Month,
'31.12.2040' AS End_Date,
'31.12.2029' AS End_Date_wp,
'2029-12-31' AS End_Date_wp_ETL,
'C' AS Project_Type,
'P003' AS Stage,
'N'                 AS Indicator__Restr__Time_Post__W_O_Staff_,
'X'                 AS Project_Invoicing_Solution,
'NA' AS Closure_Reason,
'01.01.2026' AS First_Price_Refresh_Date,
'0' AS PI_______Number,
'Yes' AS Price_Increase_PI____Indicator,
'0SAP_RL_005' AS Project_Role_ID,
'RE' AS Partner_Function,
v2.*
FROM
(
SELECT DISTINCT Service_Contract,
sold_to_party,
--REVERSE(SUBSTRING(REVERSE(sold_to_party),CHARINDEX(')', REVERSE(sold_to_party)) + 1,CHARINDEX('(',REVERSE(sold_to_party))-2)) sold_to_party_num,
sold_to_party AS sold_to_party_num,
[Description___ID] AS Project_Name,
[Employee_Responsible] AS Project_Partner_ID_ETL,
sales_organization AS Sales_Organization,
sales_organization AS Company_Code,
STR(SUM(CAST(Gross_value AS FLOAT)) OVER (PARTITION BY Service_Contract),30,2) AS ACV_Value
FROM 
[dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_SC_HEADER] h
) H
INNER JOIN
(
SELECT 'ORIGINAL' SRC,V2.* FROM [dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_SC_V2_FILTER_V] V2 
UNION ALL
SELECT 'DRE' SRC,DRE.* FROM [dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_SC_DRE_V] DRE 
UNION ALL
SELECT 'BUDDY' B,* FROM [dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_SC_BUDDY_V] B 
) V2
ON H.Service_Contract=v2.Transaction_ID
LEFT OUTER JOIN DBO.SAP_IN_CUSTOMER_XREF xref
ON H.sold_to_party_num = xref.customer_old
) B
LEFT OUTER JOIN 
(
SELECT transaction_id,Item_Number_in_Doc_, CRM__Order_Quantity,Name_for_Date_Rule,
CASE WHEN Name_for_Date_Rule = 'BILL0004' THEN 'Quarterly'
     WHEN Name_for_Date_Rule = 'BILL0007' THEN 'Annually'
     WHEN Name_for_Date_Rule = 'BILL0006' THEN 'Half Yearly'
     WHEN Name_for_Date_Rule = 'BILL0008' THEN 'Tri-Annually'
     ELSE 'Monthly'
END frequency
FROM [dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_SC_BILLING]
WHERE CAST(CRM__Order_Quantity AS FLOAT) <> 0
--AND Billing_Status <> 'C'
) BILLING
ON B.Transaction_ID=billing.Transaction_ID AND
B.Item_Number_in_Doc_key = billing.Item_Number_in_Doc_
WHERE Customer_ID IS NOT NULL;

END

GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_VIEWPINT_BILLING_PRC]    Script Date: 11/24/2025 4:05:16 PM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_VIEWPINT_BILLING_PRC]
AS
BEGIN

SET NOCOUNT ON;

DECLARE
@p1 VARCHAR(100),@p2 VARCHAR(100),@p3 VARCHAR(100),@p4 VARCHAR(100),@p5 VARCHAR(100),@p6 VARCHAR(100),
@p7 VARCHAR(100),@p8 VARCHAR(100),@p9 VARCHAR(100),@p10 VARCHAR(100),@p11 VARCHAR(100),@p12 VARCHAR(100);

DECLARE VP_CURSOR CURSOR FOR 
SELECT 
commercial_project_id, --1,
item_number_of_the_SD_document,--2
'dummy_sequence' dummy_seq, --3,
'dummy_billing_date' dummy_billing_date, --4,
CASE WHEN sales_document_item_category IN ('PS02','PS07') THEN 1
     WHEN sales_document_item_category IN ('PS01','PS06') THEN
            CASE WHEN charge_per IN ('Two Months') THEN ROUND(total_fee/2,2)
            WHEN charge_per IN ('Four Months') THEN ROUND(total_fee/4,2)
	        WHEN charge_per IN ('Semi-Annually') THEN ROUND(total_fee/6,2)
	        ELSE total_fee
            END
END AS Net_Value_in_Document_Currency,--5
CAST(SUBSTRING(CASE WHEN SRC = 'DRE' THEN start_date_wp_etl ELSE fromdate END,1,10) AS DATE) Service_Start_Date_ETL,--6
--DATEADD(YEAR,1,CAST(SUBSTRING(CASE WHEN SRC = 'DRE' THEN start_date_wp_etl ELSE fromdate END,1,10) AS DATE)) Service_Start_Date_ETL,
CAST(SUBSTRING(CASE WHEN charge_per = 'One Off' THEN todate  ELSE end_date_wp_etl END,1,10) AS DATE) Service_End_Date_ETL,--7
material_number,--8
wp_description,--9
sales_document_item_category,--10
src,--11,
charge_per --12
--start_date_wp_etl,fromdate,todate,charge_per,total_fee
FROM 
dbo.SAP_IN_PROJECT_VIEWPOINT_STG;
--WHERE CHARGE_PER='Monthly' and commercial_project_id = 'M110000507' AND Item_Number_of_the_SD_Document='3';

TRUNCATE TABLE [dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_VIEWPOINT_BILLING];

OPEN VP_CURSOR;

FETCH NEXT FROM VP_CURSOR INTO @P1,@P2,@P3,@P4,@P5,@P6,@P7,@P8,@P9,@P10,@P11,@P12;

WHILE @@FETCH_STATUS = 0
BEGIN

	IF @P12 IN ('One Off')
	BEGIN
	      INSERT INTO [dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_VIEWPOINT_BILLING]
		  SELECT @P1,@P2,'1',@P6,@P5,@P6,@P7,@P8,@P9,@P10,@P11,@P12;
	END

   ELSE IF @P12 IN ('Annually')
	BEGIN
     WITH DateList AS (
       SELECT CAST(@P6 AS DATE) AS START_DT
       UNION ALL
       SELECT DATEADD(YEAR, 1, START_DT)
       FROM DateList
       WHERE CAST(START_DT AS DATE) < CAST(@P7 AS DATE)
     )
     INSERT INTO [dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_VIEWPOINT_BILLING]
	 SELECT @P1,@P2,'1',START_DT,@P5,START_DT,DATEADD(DAY,-1,DATEADD(YEAR, 1, START_DT)),@P8,@P9,@P10,@P11,@P12
     FROM DateList
	 WHERE DATEADD(DAY,-1,DATEADD(YEAR, 1, START_DT)) <= CAST(@P7 AS DATE)
    OPTION (MAXRECURSION 0);
	END 
	ELSE IF @P12 IN ('Quarterly')
	BEGIN
     WITH DateList AS (
       SELECT CAST(@P6 AS DATE) AS START_DT
       UNION ALL
       SELECT DATEADD(QUARTER, 1, START_DT)
       FROM DateList
       WHERE CAST(START_DT AS DATE) < CAST(@P7 AS DATE)
     )
     INSERT INTO [dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_VIEWPOINT_BILLING]
	 SELECT @P1,@P2,'1',DATEADD(DAY,-1,DATEADD(QUARTER, 1, START_DT)),@P5,START_DT,DATEADD(DAY,-1,DATEADD(QUARTER, 1, START_DT)),@P8,@P9,@P10,@P11,@P12
     FROM DateList
	 WHERE DATEADD(DAY,-1,DATEADD(QUARTER, 1, START_DT)) <= CAST(@P7 AS DATE)
    OPTION (MAXRECURSION 0);
	END

   ELSE --Monthly, 2 Months, 4 Months, semi-Annually
	BEGIN
     WITH DateList AS (
       SELECT CAST(@P6 AS DATE) AS START_DT
       UNION ALL
       SELECT DATEADD(MONTH, 1, START_DT)
       FROM DateList
       WHERE CAST(START_DT AS DATE) < CAST(@P7 AS DATE)
     )
     INSERT INTO [dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_VIEWPOINT_BILLING]
	 SELECT @P1,@P2,'1',DATEADD(DAY,-1,DATEADD(MONTH, 1, START_DT)),@P5,START_DT,DATEADD(DAY,-1,DATEADD(MONTH, 1, START_DT)),@P8,@P9,@P10,@P11,@P12
     FROM DateList
	 WHERE DATEADD(DAY,-1,DATEADD(MONTH, 1, START_DT)) <= CAST(@P7 AS DATE)
    OPTION (MAXRECURSION 0);

	END

FETCH NEXT FROM VP_CURSOR INTO @P1,@P2,@P3,@P4,@P5,@P6,@P7,@P8,@P9,@P10,@P11,@P12;

END

CLOSE VP_CURSOR;
DEALLOCATE VP_CURSOR;

END
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_VIEWPOINT_PRC]    Script Date: 11/24/2025 4:05:16 PM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE         PROCEDURE [dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_VIEWPOINT_PRC] 
AS

BEGIN

TRUNCATE TABLE dbo.SAP_IN_PROJECT_VIEWPOINT_STG;

--drop table dbo.SAP_IN_PROJECT_VIEWPOINT_STG;

INSERT INTO dbo.SAP_IN_PROJECT_VIEWPOINT_STG
SELECT 
COUNT(*) OVER (PARTITION BY Commercial_Project_ID,Work_Package_Name_ETL) work_package_dup,
CAST(DENSE_RANK() OVER (PARTITION BY Commercial_Project_ID ORDER BY Work_Package_Name_ETL,material_number)  AS VARCHAR(100))   AS Sequence_Number,
CAST(DENSE_RANK() OVER (PARTITION BY Commercial_Project_ID ORDER BY Work_Package_Name_ETL,material_number)  AS VARCHAR(100))   AS Item_Number_of_the_SD_Document--,
--CAST(DENSE_RANK() OVER (PARTITION BY Commercial_Project_ID ORDER BY Billing_Due_Date)  AS VARCHAR(100))   AS Item_for_Billing_Plan_Invoice_Plan_Paym,
,a.*
--INTO dbo.SAP_IN_PROJECT_VIEWPOINT_STG
FROM (
SELECT DISTINCT 
       vp.src,
	   'M1'+vp.Master_File_Code AS Commercial_Project_ID,
        vp.Master_File_Code,
		vp.send_invoice_to,
		vp.projects,
		CASE WHEN vp.item_category IN ('PS07') THEN 'U' ELSE NULL END AS WP_Type,
		CASE WHEN vp.item_category IN ('PS07') THEN 'U003' ELSE NULL END AS Service_ID,
		CASE WHEN vp.item_category IN ('PS07') THEN '1' ELSE NULL END AS Service_Quantity,
		CONVERT(VARCHAR,
		MIN(CAST(SUBSTRING(FromDate,1,10) AS DATE)) OVER (PARTITION BY Master_File_Code)
		,104) AS Start_Date,
	    CONVERT(VARCHAR,CAST(SUBSTRING(FromDate,1,10) AS DATE),104) AS Start_Date_wp,
		FromDate AS Start_Date_wp_ETL,
	   CONVERT(VARCHAR,CAST(SUBSTRING(NextDate,1,10) AS DATE),104) AS Billing_Due_Date,
	    CASE WHEN LEFT(Rdescription,58) IS NULL THEN Master_File_Code ELSE LEFT(Rdescription,58) END AS Work_Package_Name_ETL,
		CASE WHEN vp.Master_File_Code <> vp.send_invoice_to OR vp.Master_File_Code <> vp.projects 
		THEN  'YES' ELSE 'NO' END SO_Header_Partner_flag,
		CASE WHEN vp.Master_File_Code = vp.projects THEN xref2.CUSTOMER_NEW 
		     WHEN vp.Master_File_Code = vp.send_invoice_to THEN xref.CUSTOMER_NEW 
		END AS Customer,
	   'M1'+vp.New_S4_product AS Material_Number,
	   vp.item_category AS Sales_Document_Item_Category,
       xref.CUSTOMER_NEW  AS Customer_ID,
	   CONVERT(VARCHAR,YEAR(CAST(SUBSTRING(FromDate,1,10) AS DATE))) Calendar_Year,
	   RIGHT('0'+MONTH(CAST(SUBSTRING(FromDate,1,10) AS DATE)),2) Calendar_Month,
       vp.RelationShip_Manager_Name,
	   vp.Senior_RelationShip_Manager_Name,
	   vp.File_Handler_Name,
       RevEntity+'901110' AS Cost_Center_ETL, --LKP (RevEntity]) Need Lookup
 	   '90100000' AS Profit_Center_ETL, --LKP ,Need Lookup (RevEntity,Cost Centre) , Many center there for the same RevEntity/Comp_code
	   Master_File_Name AS Project_Name,
	   'C' AS Project_Type,
	   'P003' AS Stage,
		'31.12.2040' AS End_Date,
		'31.12.2029' AS End_Date_wp,
		'2029-12-31' AS End_Date_wp_ETL,
		Currency AS Currency,
		RevEntity AS Service_Organization,
		RevEntity AS Company_Code,
	   'N'                 AS Indicator__Restr__Time_Post__W_O_Staff_,
       'X'                 AS Project_Invoicing_Solution,
	   CONVERT(VARCHAR,ROUND(SUM(CAST(Total_Fee AS FLOAT)) OVER (PARTITION BY Master_File_Code),2))  ACV_Value,
	   LEFT(RevEntity,2) AS CDM,
	   'NA' AS Closure_Reason,
	   '01.01.2026' AS First_Price_Refresh_Date,
	   '0' AS PI_______Number,
       'Yes' AS Price_Increase_PI____Indicator,
	   '0SAP_RL_005' AS Project_Role_ID,
	   CASE WHEN Rdescription IS NULL THEN Master_File_Code ELSE Rdescription END AS WP_Description,
	   'RE' AS Partner_Function,
	   CASE WHEN Rdescription IS NULL THEN Master_File_Code ELSE Rdescription END AS Material_Description,
      --CAST(CASE WHEN vp.item_category IN ('PS06','PS01') THEN Total_Fee_etl
	  --     WHEN  vp.item_category IN ('PS02','PS07') THEN 1
	 --   ELSE NULL
	--	   END AS VARCHAR(100)) AS Net_Value_in_Document_Currency,
		vp.Service_Country AS Price_Refresh___Country,
		--CASE WHEN vp.item_category='PS06' THEN CONVERT(VARCHAR,CAST(SUBSTRING(VP.FromDate,1,10) AS DATE),104) END AS Service_Start_Date,
		--CASE WHEN vp.item_category='PS06' THEN CONVERT(VARCHAR,CAST(SUBSTRING(VP.tODate,1,10) AS DATE),104) END AS Service_End_Date
        vp.EffectDate,
		vp.NextDate,
       --to handle data quality issue with oneoff frequency where fromdate is larger than todate, the below fix has implemented
		CASE WHEN CAST(SUBSTRING(FROMDATE,1,10) AS DATE) > CAST(SUBSTRING(TODATE,1,10) AS DATE) THEN vp.ToDate ELSE vp.FromDate END FromDate,
		CASE WHEN CAST(SUBSTRING(FROMDATE,1,10) AS DATE) > CAST(SUBSTRING(TODATE,1,10) AS DATE) THEN vp.FromDate ELSE vp.ToDate END ToDate,
		CAST(Total_Fee AS FLOAT) Total_Fee,
		Charge_Per
FROM 
(
SELECT
--SUM(CASE WHEN vp.item_category='PS06' THEN CAST(Total_Fee AS FLOAT) ELSE 0 END) OVER (PARTITION BY Master_File_Code) AS Total_Fee_ETL,
VP.*
FROM 
(
SELECT  'ORIGINAL' SRC,* FROM [dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_VP_EXTRACT_FILTER_V] 
 UNION ALL 
 SELECT 'DRE' SRC,* FROM [dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_VP_DRE_DUMMY_V] 
 UNION ALL
 SELECT 'BUDDY' SRC,* FROM DBO.SAP_IN_PROJECT_VP_BUDDY_V 
)vp
) vp
LEFT OUTER JOIN 
dbo.SAP_IN_CUSTOMER_XREF xref
ON vp.Master_File_Code = xref.CUSTOMER_OLD 
LEFT OUTER JOIN 
dbo.SAP_IN_CUSTOMER_XREF xref2
ON vp.Send_Invoice_to = xref2.CUSTOMER_OLD 
)A 
WHERE Customer_ID IS NOT NULL;

END


GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP]    Script Date: 11/24/2025 4:05:16 PM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO


CREATE       PROCEDURE [dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP] 
@p_filter_keyword NVARCHAR(1000)
AS
BEGIN

TRUNCATE TABLE  dbo.SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP2_TMP0;
TRUNCATE TABLE  dbo.SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_TMP1;
TRUNCATE TABLE  dbo.SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_TMP2;
--TRUNCATE TABLE  dbo.SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_DRIVER;

WITH WP AS
(
SELECT 
CAST(DENSE_RANK() OVER (PARTITION BY Commericial_Project_id_Old 
                        ORDER BY Commericial_Project_id_Old,bill_to_key,currency_key,Execution_Country_key,category_key
          			    )  AS VARCHAR(100))  new_project_number,
w.*
FROM
(
SELECT DISTINCT 
       wp.[Project_Definition]  AS Commericial_Project_id_Old,
       wp.Work_Package_WBS, 
	   wp.[Work_Package_WBS_Desc],
	   COALESCE(bill_to,'0') AS bill_to_key,
	   COALESCE(currency,'0') AS currency_key,
       CASE WHEN a.category IS NOT NULL THEN 'G1' 
	        WHEN a.category IS NULL AND wp.Execution_Country IS NOT NULL THEN wp.Execution_Country
			WHEN a.category IS NULL AND wp.Execution_Country IS NULL THEN LEFT(wp.Company_Code,2) 
			END AS Execution_Country_Key,
	   COALESCE(a.category,'0') category_key,
	   UPPER(COALESCE(product, '0')) as product_key, 
	   CASE WHEN a.product_advisory IS NOT NULL THEN '1' ELSE '0' END AS advisory_flag_key,
	   CASE WHEN a.category IS NOT NULL AND UPPER(a.category)='LEGAL' THEN '1' ELSE 0 END legal_exists_flag,
	   CASE WHEN a.category IS NOT NULL AND UPPER(a.category)='TAX'   THEN '1' ELSE 0 END tax_exists_flag,
	   CASE WHEN a.category IS NOT NULL AND UPPER(a.category)='HR'    THEN '1' ELSE 0 END hr_exists_flag,
	   CASE WHEN CHARINDEX('DRE', UPPER(COALESCE(product_1, '0')))>0 THEN '1' ELSE 0 END dre_exists_flag,
	   CASE WHEN b.action = 'FILTER' THEN '1' ELSE 0 END prd_filter_flag
FROM 
[dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_WORK_PACKAGE] wp
INNER JOIN
(
   SELECT *--P1.Project-- , p1.Project_Name,p1.end_date
   FROM [dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_PROF_SERVICES] P1
   WHERE P1.Current_Stage NOT IN ('Closed','Completed') AND
         (UPPER(P1.Company_code)  NOT LIKE '%CN07%' AND UPPER(P1.Company_code)   NOT LIKE 'ZZ%') AND
		 P1.Project  IN (SELECT project_name FROM [dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_FILTER] WHERE comment LIKE '%'+@p_filter_keyword+'%') AND
		 UPPER(p1.Project_Name) NOT LIKE '%CLOSED%' AND UPPER(TRIM(p1.Project_Name)) NOT LIKE '%DONOTUSE%' AND
		 CAST(p1.End_Date AS DATE) > CAST('2024-12-31' AS DATE) 
) P1
ON wp.Project_Definition = P1.project
LEFT OUTER JOIN DBO.SAP_IN_PROJECT_PRODUCT_ADVISORY A
ON wp.PRODUCT = A.PRODUCT_ADVISORY
LEFT OUTER JOIN dbo.sap_in_project_product_bridge b
ON wp.PRODUCT = B.PRODUCT_OLD
WHERE 
wp.Stage NOT IN ('P004','P005') AND  
wp.Product IS NOT NULL AND
--wp.PRODUCT NOT IN (SELECT PRODUCT FROM DBO.SAP_IN_PROJECT_PRODUCT_REMOVE ) AND
CAST(wp.Work_Package_End_Date AS DATE) > CAST('2024-12-31' AS DATE) AND
UPPER(Work_Package_Name) NOT LIKE '%CLOSED%' 
) w
),
WP1 AS
(
SELECT 'M1'+Commericial_Project_id_Old+'A'+new_project_number AS Commericial_Project_id_new, WP.*,
MAX(dre_exists_flag) OVER (PARTITION BY Commericial_Project_id_Old,new_project_number) AS dre_exists_group_flag,
MAX(prd_filter_flag) OVER (PARTITION BY Commericial_Project_id_Old,new_project_number) AS prd_filter_group_flag
FROM WP 
),
WP2 AS
(--Everything
SELECT * FROM WP1 WHERE prd_filter_group_flag <> 1
) 
INSERT INTO dbo.SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP2_TMP0
SELECT * FROM WP2;

WITH WP2 AS
(
SELECT * FROM SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP2_TMP0
),
WP3_LEGAL AS
(
SELECT Commericial_Project_id_Old,Commericial_Project_id_new,MAX(work_package_wbs) work_package_wbs,clone.src
FROM WP2
CROSS JOIN 
(SELECT 'ORIGINAL' SRC UNION ALL SELECT 'CLONE_LEGAL' SRC) clone
WHERE advisory_flag_key=1 and legal_exists_flag = 1 
GROUP BY Commericial_Project_id_Old,Commericial_Project_id_new, clone.src
),
WP3_TAX AS
(
SELECT Commericial_Project_id_Old,Commericial_Project_id_new,MAX(work_package_wbs) work_package_wbs,clone.src
FROM WP2
CROSS JOIN 
(SELECT 'ORIGINAL' SRC UNION ALL SELECT 'CLONE_TAX' SRC) clone
WHERE advisory_flag_key=1 and tax_exists_flag = 1 
GROUP BY Commericial_Project_id_Old,Commericial_Project_id_new, clone.src
),
WP3_HR AS
(
SELECT Commericial_Project_id_Old,Commericial_Project_id_new,MAX(work_package_wbs) work_package_wbs,clone.src
FROM WP2
CROSS JOIN 
(SELECT 'ORIGINAL' SRC UNION ALL SELECT 'CLONE_HR1' SRC UNION ALL SELECT 'CLONE_HR2' ) clone
WHERE advisory_flag_key=1 and hr_exists_flag = 1 
GROUP BY Commericial_Project_id_Old,Commericial_Project_id_new, clone.src
),
WP3_DRE AS
(
SELECT Commericial_Project_id_Old,Commericial_Project_id_new,MAX(work_package_wbs) work_package_wbs,clone.src
FROM WP2
CROSS JOIN 
(SELECT 'ORIGINAL' SRC UNION ALL SELECT 'CLONE_DRE' SRC) clone
WHERE dre_exists_group_flag <> 1 
GROUP BY Commericial_Project_id_Old,Commericial_Project_id_new, clone.src
),
WP3_BUDDY AS
(
SELECT Commericial_Project_id_Old,Commericial_Project_id_new,work_package_wbs,x2.SRC 
FROM WP2 x1
INNER JOIN
SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_BUDDY x2 ON
x1.product_key = x2.JOIN_KEY
),
WP3_DEFAULT_ONLY AS
(
SELECT * FROM WP3_LEGAL
UNION 
SELECT * FROM WP3_TAX
UNION 
SELECT * FROM WP3_HR
UNION 
SELECT * FROM WP3_DRE
UNION 
SELECT * FROM WP3_BUDDY WHERE work_package_wbs IN (SELECT MAX(b.work_package_wbs)
                               FROM WP3_BUDDY b
							   WHERE b.src LIKE 'CLONE_BUDDY%'
							   GROUP BY b.Commericial_Project_id_new,b.SRC
							   )
) 
INSERT INTO dbo.SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_TMP1
SELECT * FROM WP3_DEFAULT_ONLY OPTION (RECOMPILE,FORCE ORDER, MAXDOP 10);

WITH WP2 AS
(
SELECT * FROM SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP2_TMP0
),
WP3_LEGAL AS
(
SELECT Commericial_Project_id_Old,Commericial_Project_id_new,MAX(work_package_wbs) work_package_wbs,clone.src
FROM WP2
CROSS JOIN 
(SELECT 'ORIGINAL' SRC UNION ALL SELECT 'CLONE_LEGAL' SRC) clone
WHERE advisory_flag_key=1 and legal_exists_flag = 1 
GROUP BY Commericial_Project_id_Old,Commericial_Project_id_new, clone.src
),
WP3_TAX AS
(
SELECT Commericial_Project_id_Old,Commericial_Project_id_new,MAX(work_package_wbs) work_package_wbs,clone.src
FROM WP2
CROSS JOIN 
(SELECT 'ORIGINAL' SRC UNION ALL SELECT 'CLONE_TAX' SRC) clone
WHERE advisory_flag_key=1 and tax_exists_flag = 1 
GROUP BY Commericial_Project_id_Old,Commericial_Project_id_new, clone.src
),
WP3_HR AS
(
SELECT Commericial_Project_id_Old,Commericial_Project_id_new,MAX(work_package_wbs) work_package_wbs,clone.src
FROM WP2
CROSS JOIN 
(SELECT 'ORIGINAL' SRC UNION ALL SELECT 'CLONE_HR1' SRC UNION ALL SELECT 'CLONE_HR2' ) clone
WHERE advisory_flag_key=1 and hr_exists_flag = 1 
GROUP BY Commericial_Project_id_Old,Commericial_Project_id_new, clone.src
),
WP3_DRE AS
(
SELECT Commericial_Project_id_Old,Commericial_Project_id_new,MAX(work_package_wbs) work_package_wbs,clone.src
FROM WP2
CROSS JOIN 
(SELECT 'ORIGINAL' SRC UNION ALL SELECT 'CLONE_DRE' SRC) clone
WHERE dre_exists_group_flag <> 1 
GROUP BY Commericial_Project_id_Old,Commericial_Project_id_new, clone.src
),
WP3_BUDDY AS
(
SELECT Commericial_Project_id_Old,Commericial_Project_id_new,work_package_wbs,x2.SRC 
FROM WP2 x1
INNER JOIN
SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_BUDDY x2 ON
x1.product_key = x2.JOIN_KEY
),
WP3_DEFAULT_ONLY AS
(
SELECT * FROM WP3_LEGAL
UNION 
SELECT * FROM WP3_TAX
UNION 
SELECT * FROM WP3_HR
UNION 
SELECT * FROM WP3_DRE
UNION 
SELECT * FROM WP3_BUDDY WHERE work_package_wbs IN (SELECT MAX(b.work_package_wbs)
                               FROM WP3_BUDDY b
							   WHERE b.src LIKE 'CLONE_BUDDY%'
							   GROUP BY b.Commericial_Project_id_new,b.SRC
							   )
), 
WP3_WITHOUT_DEFAULT AS
(
SELECT Commericial_Project_id_Old,Commericial_Project_id_new,work_package_wbs,'ORIGINAL' SRC 
FROM
WP2 x WHERE x.Work_Package_WBS NOT IN (SELECT DISTINCT y.Work_Package_WBS FROM WP3_DEFAULT_ONLY y)
) 
INSERT INTO dbo.SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_TMP2
SELECT * FROM WP3_WITHOUT_DEFAULT OPTION (RECOMPILE,FORCE ORDER, MAXDOP 10);


WITH ALL_DATA AS
(
SELECT * FROM SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_TMP1
UNION 
SELECT * FROM SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_TMP2
) 
INSERT INTO dbo.SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_DRIVER 
SELECT z.*,CAST(DENSE_RANK() OVER (PARTITION BY commericial_project_id_old ORDER BY work_package_wbs)  AS VARCHAR(100))   AS sequence_number_etl_join,
CAST(DENSE_RANK() OVER (PARTITION BY commericial_project_id_new ORDER BY work_package_wbs,src)  AS VARCHAR(100))   AS sequence_number_group_etl_join,
CONVERT(VARCHAR(100), GETDATE(), 120) AS ENTRY_DATE,
'Y' Active_flag
FROM ALL_DATA z
WHERE Z.Commericial_Project_id_Old NOT IN (SELECT i.Commericial_Project_id_Old FROM dbo.SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_DRIVER i)
OPTION (RECOMPILE,FORCE ORDER, MAXDOP 10);

END;


GO
USE [master]
GO
ALTER DATABASE [SAP_DM_DEV] SET  READ_WRITE 
GO
